Ban Long Wan
Strengthens the spirit, eliminates numerous ailments, nourishes qi and blood, repairs various injuries, and promotes offspring, showing remarkable effects. Elderly and weak individuals should take it regularly for longevity. In the past, there was a Daoist in Shu who sang joyfully in a tavern: "The tailbone cannot restrain the endless sea, and even the nine transformations of the golden elixir are slowly discussed. Only the pearl atop Ban Long can replenish the blood beneath the jade hall." The true person Zhong Yuan sought the formula to pass on to the world.

Ingredients:
Lu Jiao Shuang, Lu Jiao Jiao, and Tu Si Zi, each half a jin; Bai Zi Ren and Shu Di Huang, each four liang; Bai Fu Ling and Bu Gu Zhi, each four liang.
Dissolve the gelatin first, combine with ash-free wine to make a paste, and form pills the size of Wutong seeds. Take six to seventy pills on an empty stomach, with salt water or wine as preferred.[36p]

Taiji Pill: Fills essence and nourishes marrow, prolonging life. The five organs of man correspond to the five elements of heaven and earth. Any discord leads to illness. Medicinal substances possess five flavors, each governing a specific organ; they should be proportionally adjusted, harmonizing all flavors to support the spirit and energy of heart and kidney, maintaining balance without loss. When the source of transformation is clear, evil cannot intrude, hence it is called Taiji. Yellow bitter (peel removed, seasoned with salt and wine until brown, then ground to a fine powder, three taels and six qians), anemarrhena (hair removed, soaked in wine overnight, lightly fried, ground to a fine powder, three taels and four qians), fried paper and new tiles for fragrance (ground to a fine powder, two taels and eight qians), walnut kernels (peeled and ground, three taels and two qians), cardamom (one tael, divided into two parts: one part fried with five qians of prickly ash, the other used raw). Grind the right side into fine powder, form into honey pills the size of a phoenix tree seed. Take five to seventy pills each time, morning and evening with boiling soup or tea. After three years of continuous use, all ailments will be eliminated. Taking it throughout life without interruption can lead to becoming an earthly immortal.[37p]

有赤白浊，加白朮、白茯苓各二两半，山栀仁炒、黄连炒各半两。脚膝软弱无力，加牛膝酒洗、虎骨酥炙各二两，防己酒洗、木瓜各半两。疝气加苍朮盐炒两半，黄连姜汁炒、山栀仁炒各六钱，川芎一两，吴茱萸炮、青皮各半两。脾胃虚弱，胃寒易泄，加白朮三两，陈皮一两，干姜炮七钱。眼目昏暗，加当归酒洗、川芎、菊花各二两，柴胡、黄连酒炒、乌犀各半两，蔓荆子、防风各三钱。气虚之人，加人参、黄芪炙各二两。左尺既虚，右尺亦微，命门火衰，阳事不举，加肉桂、黑附子制各七钱，沉香五钱。[39p]

　　人参固本丸 【《千金方》】 　夫人心藏血，肾藏精，精血充实，则须发不白，颜色不衰，老而有子，延年益寿。其夭者，多由服热药，不能滋生精血。而药之补精血者，无出于生熟二地黄。世人徒知服二地黄，而不知服二门冬为引。盖生地黄能生心血，用麦门冬引入所生之地；熟地黄能补肾精，用天门冬引入所补之地。四味互相为用，《本草》又以人参为通心气之主，故加之。　　生地黄　熟地黄各酒浸　天门冬酒浸去心　麦门冬酒浸去心，各二两　人参一两　　右为末，炼蜜为丸梧桐子大，每服五十丸，空心，温酒盐汤任下。如有痰者，二地黄俱用姜汁炒过，恐滞膈故也。[41p]

Ginseng Guardian Pill 【from Essential Prescriptions】

The heart contains blood, and the kidneys store essence. When essence and blood are abundant, hair remains unturned gray, complexion remains vibrant, one can still father children in old age, thereby prolonging life. Premature aging often results from the overuse of warming medicines that fail to nourish essence and blood. Among medicines that replenish essence and blood, the two Dihuang herbs (raw and cooked) stand out. People often know to take the two Dihuang herbs but fail to recognize that Asparagus Racemosus serves as a guide for their effects. Raw Dihuang can nourish heart blood, with Ophiopogon Japonicus directing this nourishment; cooked Dihuang can replenish kidney essence, with another Asparagus guiding this replenishment. These four ingredients work synergistically. The Herbal Classic additionally emphasizes Ginseng as a primary agent for harmonizing heart energy, hence its inclusion.

Ingredients:

  • 120g raw Dihuang (soaked in wine)
  • 120g cooked Dihuang (soaked in wine)
  • 120g Ophiopogon (soaked in wine and heart removed)
  • 120g Asparagus (soaked in wine and heart removed)
  • 30g Ginseng

Grind these into powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of a nut. Take 50 pills on an empty stomach, followed by warm wine or saline soup as desired. If phlegm is present, both types of Dihuang should be stir-fried with ginger juice to prevent blockage in the diaphragm.[41p]

　　三才封髓丹　降心火，益肾水，久服多子。　　天门冬　熟地黄　人参各半两　砂仁炒，两半　黄蘗炒褐色，三两　甘草炙，七钱　　右为末，面糊丸梧桐子大，每服五十丸，以肉苁蓉五钱切片，酒浸一宿，次日煎三四沸，去渣，空心送丸子。
　　固真丹　治诸虚百损，五劳七伤，水火不升降，下元虚冷无子，脐腹痛。　　熟地黄四两，酒煮捣膏　人参　山药　当归　黄芪　黄蘗制　白朮　杜仲　故纸炒，各一两　五味子　白茯苓　丹皮　山萸肉　泽泻各半两　　右为细末，和地黄膏搜匀，入炼蜜和丸梧桐子大，每服八十丸，空心淡盐汤送下。腰腿无力，加牛膝一两酒炒，龟板两半酥炙。夏天加龟板半两。脉弱食少，再加附子半两。[42p]

Quan Lu Wan (Whole Deer Pills)

This medicine can replenish all deficiencies and injuries, remedying the five labors and seven damages; its effects cannot be fully described. If four individuals jointly prepare a single dose and consume it, it can prolong life and increase descendants. The method involves four people collaborating to process one deer, and then they divide and consume it. After a year, they can prepare it again, and if they do this for four years, each person will end up with a whole deer. However, if one person tries to prepare a single dose alone, it may spoil over time, and the medicinal potency will diminish.

For preparing the deer, take one pair of deer (there's no restriction on gender), bind them and slaughter them, remove the fur and internal organs, then wash them clean and render them into a paste. The deer meat should be cooked thoroughly, sliced, and dried into powder; the skin should be mixed in with a basic broth to create a paste, which is then combined with the powdered medicine to form pills. The bones should be ground into powder and mixed together with the meat powder and medicinal powder, kneaded with glue.[50p]

不成丸，加蜜　人参　黄芪　白朮　茯苓　生地　破故纸　巴戟天　当归　川芎　熟地　天冬　麦冬　陈皮　炙 甘草　枸杞子　续断　杜仲　牛膝　琐阳　秋石　葫卢巴　干山药　芡实子　菟丝子　五味子　覆盆子　楮实子　肉苁蓉各一斤　川椒去目子并闭口炒去汗　小茴香　青盐　沉香各半斤　　右各精制为末，各称分两，和匀一处，候鹿制胶成，就和为丸，梧桐子大，焙干，用生黄绢作小袋五十条，每条约盛一斤，悬置透风处。用尽一袋，又取一袋。霉伏天须要火烘一二次为妙。每服八九十丸，空心，临卧时，姜汤、盐汤、沸汤任下，冬月温酒送下。[51p]

Not made into pills, add honey: ginseng, astragalus, white atractylodes, poria, raw rhubarb, broken old paper, morinda root, angelica, ligusticum, cooked rehmannia, tian dong, mai dong, dried tangerine peel, roasted licorice, goji berries, jujube, eucommia, achyranthes, sutra stone, hulu ba, dried yam, fox nut seeds, dodder seeds, schisandra, raspberry, mulberry seeds, and piece of cistanche, each one pound. Remove seeds from sichuan pepper and stir-fry to sweat out moisture. Small fennel, blue salt, and agarwood, each half a pound.

All the above are finely ground into powder, weighed out and mixed evenly. When the deer gelatin is prepared, combine into pills the size of a Phoenix seed, roast dry, using raw yellow silk to make fifty small bags, each holding about one pound, and hang them in a breezy place. Once a bag is used, take another bag. During humid days, lightly heat in the fire once or twice for best results. Take eight to ninety pills on an empty stomach, just before bedtime, and wash down with ginger soup, salty water, or boiling water as preferred, using warm wine in the winter.[51p]

　　雀卵菟丝丸　助阳固精，最为奇效。此方纯正，久服有益无损。视之桂、附、麝、沉等药，助阳取效一时，久则致火，大有间矣。　　菟丝子二斤，重汤酒煮三日夜，汁干用石臼杵捣为泥块，作饼子炕干为细末，酒糊丸作饼子晒干　雀卵一百枚，去黄用白，和菟丝净末一斤　　右炼蜜为丸，梧桐子大，空心酒下七十丸。[52p]

The Sparrow Egg Cuscuta Pill enhances yang and solidifies essence, proving to be exceptionally effective. This formula is pure and beneficial when taken over a long period, with no harmful effects. Compared to herbs like cinnamon, aconite, musk, and agarwood, which may boost yang for a time but can lead to excess fire if taken too long, this formulation is safer.

Use two pounds of Cuscuta seeds, boil them for three days and nights in heavy liquor, then drain and grind the mixture into a paste using a stone mortar and pestle. Form the paste into cakes and dry them into a fine powder. Take one hundred sparrow eggs, remove the yolks and use only the whites, mixing them with one pound of the purified Cuscuta powder.

Finally, prepare honey into pills the size of phoenix tree seeds, making seventy hollow pills, to be taken with liquor.[52p]

　　御米酒　壮筋骨，畅经络，养精元，益神气。久服行步如飞，延年益嗣，有通仙之妙。　　真薏苡米酒一百斤　霜茄根切片　五加皮切　真桑寄生銼　苍耳子炒去刺，各半斤　枸杞子　牛膝去芦，各一斤　　右各制净，称分两，每味分四剂，酒一百斤，亦分四坛，各入药煮三炷香，取放土地上，退火性。一七可饮，久窨尤佳。早晚随量饮，微醺为度。此药虽平易有奇效，不可以其简而忽之。

Secret Recipe for the Bān Lóng Er Zhì Bǎi Bǔ Wán

This medicine consolidates the foundation and preserves the original essence, promotes vitality and nourishes the blood, restores the natural state, and greatly replenishes deficiencies. It benefits the five internal organs and alleviates bone steaming, strengthens the yang and increases offspring, enriches the blood vessels, strengthens the sinews and bones, beautifies the complexion, prolongs life, sharpens the senses, nourishes the beard and mustache, truly a remarkable and extraordinary formula, difficult to fully describe its wondrous effects.

Ingredients:

  • 50 taels of deer antler (preferably freshly collected with the brain bone), sawed into two-inch lengths, washed in running water, soaked in rice water overnight, cleaned and dried; along with the following:
  • 8 taels of polygonatum,
  • 4 taels each of goji berries, cooked rehmannia, and cuscus grass (washed in hot water);
  • 4 taels of jujube seeds (fur removed),
  • 2 taels each of tian-dong (with heart removed), mai-dong (with heart removed), niu-xi (washed in wine), and mulberry seeds (washed in water),
  • 1 tael of longan flesh.

Mix the above ten ingredients evenly, place them in a clean jar, and layer them tightly. Pour in fresh, lightly salted water until the jar is filled to the shoulder. Seal the opening with four layers of fine cloth and weigh it down with a new brick. In a large pot set on a grid, cover tightly with a wooden lid, and simmer in water for three days and nights without interruption of heat.[58p]

旁用小锅烧滚水，不时添注坛内并锅内，勿使干涸，日足取起，滤去滓，将汁用绢绞出，入净砂锅内，文火熬成膏，约一斤半，再炼蜜二斤，滴水成珠，搀入，和后项药杵烂为丸。　　鹿角霜十两　人参五两　黄芪蜜炒　鸡头粉　白茯苓去皮　山药炒　山茱萸肉盐水洗过　生地黄酒洗饭上蒸过　知母盐水炒，各四两　五味子一两，去梗　夏月加川黄蘗四两炒褐色。　　已上十味为细末，用前膏和匀成块，石臼木杵杵千余下，为丸如梧桐子大，空心，盐汤送下八十丸。随用煮熟莲子肉，或晒干枣数枚以压之，俾纳丹田也。[59p]

Use a small pot to boil water, occasionally adding to both the vat and the pot to prevent drying out. One should take it out daily, filter off the dregs, and extract the juice using fine silk, placing it into a clean sand pot. Simmer it over low heat until it turns into a paste, approximately a pound and a half. Then refine two pounds of honey until it forms droplets as large as pearls, mix it in, and grind it with the remaining ingredients into pills.

The ingredients are as follows:

  • 10 taels of deer antler frost
  • 5 taels of ginseng
  • 4 taels each of honey-fried astragalus, powdered chicken head, peeled white poria, fried Chinese yam, salt-water washed fruits of cornelian cherry, steamed with rice wine, and salt-water fried anemarrhena
  • 1 tael of schisandra, stem removed
  • In summer, add 4 taels of fried yellow bran until brown.

Grind these ten ingredients into a fine powder, mix with the earlier paste to form a block, then pound it over a thousand times in a stone mortar with a wooden pestle, shaping it into pills the size of a wutong seed, hollow inside, and take 80 pills with salt broth. Optionally, use cooked lotus seed flesh or a few dried dates to press down for easier absorption into the lower abdomen.[59p]

　　腽肭脐丸 【《济生方》，下同】 　治五劳七伤，真阳衰惫，脐腹冷痛，肢体酸痛，腰背拘急，脚膝缓弱，面色黧黑，肌肉消瘦，目眩耳鸣，口苦舌干，饮食无味，腹中虚鸣，胁下刺痛，心常惨戚，夜多异梦，昼少精神，小便滑数，大腑溏泻，时有遗沥，阳事不举。但是风虚痼冷，皆宜服之。　　腽肭脐一对，酒蒸熟和后药　川乌炮去皮尖　天雄炮去皮　附子炮去皮脐　阳起石煅　锺乳粉各二两　朱砂研细　人参　沉香不见火别碾　鹿茸酒蒸，各一两　　右为细末，用腽肭脐膏子，入少酒糊，入臼内杵和，丸如桐子大，每服七十丸，空心用盐酒盐汤任下。[60p]

Tai Ru Qi Pill

It also treats long-term issues with qi and blood, numbness in the hands and feet, hemiplegia, abnormal discharges (red or white), profuse bleeding, and abdominal pain after childbirth, along with vomiting, heart pain, and dead fetuses in the womb causing pain around the navel. It alleviates fullness and bloating, excessive sweating, menstrual irregularities, swelling and weakness in the limbs, blood depletion and weakness, incontinence, loss of speech due to stroke, locked jaws, postpartum diarrhea and thirst, hallucinations, insufficient blood flow leading to headaches, pale yellow complexion, various diseases causing dripping, excessive bleeding, bloody dysentery, lack of appetite, postpartum cold, fatigue, and weight loss after childbirth.[70p]

  • Fresh coix seeds
  • Dried yam, each 1升
  • 2升 of glutinous rice

Grind these ingredients into a powder and mix them thoroughly. Store in a single container. In summer, use 3升 of Qian Shi as the main ingredient, reducing the other flavors, as prolonged storage may cause loss of potency.

Every morning, on an empty stomach, mix a blend of the rice soup with 1-2 handfuls of the powder in a silver container until well combined, then cook until it resembles porridge, adding 2 tablespoons of white sugar. If you do not have a silver pot, a clay pot will suffice, but avoid using copper or iron pots.

This can replace your morning porridge. Do not interrupt the intake; after six months, you will notice results. There is no need for additional medicinal herbs, as nurturing the spleen and stomach will strengthen the earth element, which can nourish all things.

Essence, energy, and spirit all originate from the spleen's earth. There has never been a weak spleen that produces abundant essence. With strong earth and rich essence, naturally, there will be children.

This method seems quite simple and surpasses many other formulas. Those who have tried it report effectiveness, even continuing into old age, resulting in increased vitality.[72p]

　　八珍益母丸　专治气血两虚，脾胃并弱，饮食少思，四肢无力，月经违期，或先期而至，或腰疼腹胀，缓而不至，或愆期不收，或断或续，或赤白带下，身作寒热，服之罔不获效。一月之后，即可受胎。虚甚者用药一斤，必能对期受孕。　　益母草四两，忌铁器，止用上半节带叶者　人参　白朮土炒　茯苓　当归酒洗　炙甘草　川芎　白芍药酢炒　熟地黄酒洗，各二两　　右为末，炼蜜为丸如弹子大，空心蜜汤下一丸。如不能嚼者，丸以细粒如小豆大，每服七八十丸。脾胃虚寒者，加砂仁一两姜汁炒。腹中胀闷者，加山楂一两净肉饭上蒸。多食者，加香附子一两童便制。[73p]

Bajian Yimu Pills specifically treat both Qi and blood deficiency, weakness of the spleen and stomach, poor appetite, weakness in the limbs, irregular menstrual periods, either arriving early or delaying, back pain with abdominal distension, slow to arrive, or absent, or intermittent, or experiencing red or white discharge, with alternating cold and heat in the body. Taking this remedy will yield results without fail. After a month, one can conceive. For severe deficiencies, using a pound of the medicine will guarantee timely conception.

The ingredients are: Yimucao (four taels, avoid iron utensils, only use the upper half with leaves), ginseng, baizhu (stir-fried), fu ling, dang gui (washed with wine), roasted licorice, chuan xiong, bai shao (vinegar stir-fried), and sheng di huang (washed with wine), each two taels.

The above ingredients should be ground into a powder and mixed with honey to form pills the size of a marble. If chewing is difficult, the pills can be made into smaller pieces like small beans, with a dosage of seventy to eighty pills at a time. For those with a deficient cold spleen and stomach, add one tael of sand ginger stir-fried with ginger juice. For abdominal distension and discomfort, add one tael of hawthorn steamed with clean rice. For those who overeat, add one tael of xiangfuzi made with young urine.[73p]

　　八珍益母十全丸　资益坤元，补养气血。除淋沥带下，俾羸形体壮，坐建调经受孕之功，即如樽俎折冲。胎前和气，产后补虚，真妇女之圣剂，超古今之妙方。有室家者，不可不知也。　　益母草五月五日，或六月六日，采阴干用上半节连穗叶，忌铁器，八两　人参饭上蒸　白朮饭上蒸　白茯苓饭上蒸　白芍药酢炒，各一两　甘草炙　川芎各五钱　当归身酒浸　熟地酒浸，各二两　沉香四两　　右各为极细末，炼蜜和丸如梧桐子大，空心，蜜汤送下九十丸，食干果子压之。不善吞者，化开服尤效。冬月酒下。妇女经脉不调者，或有气血两虚，而身体素弱，服此以养血。且调当年而经不通者，服一料则通；经不调者，服一月则调；素不孕者，服一只即孕。[74p]

It is greatly beneficial for longevity and nurturing yang essence, with benefits too numerous to describe.

Phoenix Chick Pills: Take a pair of black-boned chickens (both male and female) and raise them separately, avoiding mixing with other chickens. When the eggs are laid, draw a circle at the top of the first eggs. When there are many eggs, take the first one and open the shell at the marked circle. Use three qian of realgar, along with two qian each of Angelica sinensis, peony root, chuanxiong, and cooked rehmannia, ground into powder. Pour out the yolk, mix with the medicinal powder, and place it back inside the shell. If it cannot be completely filled, use another shell as well, sealing both with thick paper and placing them among the other eggs. When the chicks hatch, take out the eggs with the medicine and remove their shells. Mix with honey and form into pills, taking them on an empty stomach with good wine; taking thirty or forty pills will lead to pregnancy. 【"Medical Compendium"】[81p]

　　《千金方》房中补益论曰：人生四十已下，多有放恣。四十已上，即顿觉气力一时衰退。衰退既至，众病蜂起，久而不治，遂至不救。所以彭祖曰：以人疗人，真得其真。故年至四十须谙房中之术。夫房中术者，其道甚近，而人莫能行。其法一夕御十人，闭固为谨，此房中之术毕矣。兼之药饵四时勿绝，则气力百倍，而智慧日新，然此方之作也，非欲务于淫佚，苟求快意，务存节欲以广养生也。非苟欲强身以淫女色，以纵情意，在补益以遣疾也。此房中之微旨也。是以人年四十已下，即服房中之药者，皆所以速祸，慎之慎之！故年未满四十者，不足与论房中之事。[82p]

Guidance

The "Thousand Gold Prescription" states: Those under forty often indulge freely. Once one surpasses forty, one immediately feels a decline in vigor. When decline sets in, numerous ailments arise; if left untreated for a long time, it leads to irreparable damage. Hence, Peng Zu said: Healing one person with another can lead to true understanding. Therefore, by the age of forty, one must be familiar with the techniques of the bedroom. The methods of these techniques are very accessible, yet few can practice them. The principle is to govern oneself like one would with ten people in a single evening, being cautious and discreet; this is the essence of the bedroom skills. Additionally, if one continuously consumes medicine throughout the seasons, vitality multiplies, and wisdom is renewed daily. However, the purpose of these practices is not to seek indulgence or fleeting pleasure; rather, it is to maintain moderation for the sake of preserving life. It is not merely for strengthening oneself through lustful pursuits or to indulge desires but to replenish and alleviate ailments. This is the subtle meaning of the bedroom techniques. Therefore, those under forty who take bedroom herbs often encounter speedy misfortunes—exercise caution! Thus, those who have not yet reached forty are not suitable to discuss matters of the bedroom.[82p]

欲心未止，兼饵补药，倍力耗丧，不过半年，精髓枯竭，惟向死近。少年极须慎之。人年四十已上，常固精养气，不耗可以不老。又饵云母，足以愈疾延年。人年四十已上，勿服泻药，常饵补药大佳。昔黄帝御女一千二百而登仙，而俗人以一女伐命，知与不知，岂不远欤？其知道者，御女苦不多耳。凡妇人不必须有颜色妍丽，但得少年，未经生乳，多肌肉益也。若足财力，选取细发，目睛黑白分明，体柔骨软，肌肤细滑，言语声音和调，四肢骨节皆欲足肉而骨不大，其体及腋皆不欲有毫，有毫尝软细，不可极于相者。但蓬头蝇面，槌项结喉，雄声大口，高鼻麦齿，目睛浑浊，口颔有毫，骨节高大，发黄少肉，隐毫多而且强，又生逆毫，此相不可，皆贼命损寿也。[83p]

Desires have not yet ceased, and combined with the consumption of tonics and medicines, one quickly exhausts their vitality within half a year, leading to a depletion of essence and bringing one closer to death. In ancient times, the Yellow Emperor took 1,200 maidens and ascended to immortality, while common people lose their life over one maiden. Those who understand this are clearly far removed from ignorance. The wise man knows that consuming too many maidens is not beneficial.

A woman does not have to possess beautiful looks but should be youthful, unblemished by childbirth, and have more muscle. If fortunate and wealthy, one should choose a woman with fine hair, distinct black and white eyes, a supple body, soft bones, smooth skin, and harmonious and gentle speech; her limbs and joints should be well-fleshed but not overly large in bone. Conversely, traits like a messy hairdo, a thick neck, a loud voice and large mouth, high nose and prominent teeth, murky eyes, facial hair, large bones, yellowish skin with little flesh, an abundance of coarse hair, and reversed hair growth are all negative signs. Such traits can steal one’s life and shorten longevity.[83p]

凡御女之道，不欲令气未感动，阳气微弱，即以交合。必须先徐徐调和，使神和意感，良久，乃可令得阴气。阴气推之，须爽自强。所谓弱而内迎，坚急出之。进退欲令疏迟，情动而止。不可高自投掷，颠倒五脏，伤绝精脉生致百病。但数交而慎密者，诸病皆愈，年寿日益，去仙不远矣。不必九一三五之数也，能百接而不施泻者长生矣。若御女多者可采气。采气之道，但深接勿动，使良久气上面热，以口相当，引取女气而吞之。可疏疏进退，意动便止。缓息瞑目，偃卧道引，身体更强，可复御他女也。数数易之，则得益多。人常御一女，阴气转弱，为益亦少。阳道法火，阴道法水。水能制火，阴亦消阳。久用不止，阴气逾伤。阳则转损，所得不补所失。[84p]

In the way of approaching women, one should not engage when the energy is unresponsive and the yang energy is weak; instead, one must first gradually harmonize, allowing the spirit and intention to connect deeply for a long while before achieving the yin energy. The yin energy must be pushed, firm yet gentle. It is said that one should be weak yet receptive, strong yet resolute in action. If one has many partners, they can gather energy. The method of gathering energy is simply to connect deeply without movement, allowing the energy to rise and warm up for a long time. Breathe slowly, close the eyes, relax the body, allowing for greater strength, thus being able to engage with other women as well. By alternating partners, one can gain many benefits.

If one frequently engages with one woman, the yin energy weakens and the benefits diminish. The yang pathway follows the nature of fire, while the yin follows that of water. Water can extinguish fire, and the yin can also dissipate the yang. If engaged in excessively, the yin energy becomes overly depleted. 但能御十二女而不复施泻者，令人不老，有美色。若御九十三女而自固者，年万岁矣。凡精少则病，精尽则死。不可不思，不可不慎。数交而一泻，精气随长，不能使人虚也。若不数交，交而即泻，则不得益。泻之精气，自然生长。但迟微不如数交接不泻之速也。凡人习交合之时，常以鼻多内气，口微吐气，自然益矣。交会毕蒸热，是得气也。以菖蒲末三分，白粱粉傅磨令燥，既使强盛，又湿疮不生也。凡欲施泻者，当闭口张目闭气，握固两手，左右上下，缩鼻取气，又缩下部，及吸腹小偃脊膂，急以左手中指掩抑屏翳穴，长吐气，并琢齿千遍，则精上补脑，使人长生。若精妄出则损神也。《仙经》曰：令人长生不老，先与女戏饮玉浆。玉浆，口中津也。[85p]

使男女感动，以左手握持，思存丹田中，有赤气内黄外白，变为日月，徘徊丹田中，俱入泥垣，两半合成一咽，闭气深内，勿出入，但上下徐徐咽气。情动欲出，急退之。此非上士有智者，不能行也。其丹田在脐下三寸。泥垣者在头中对两目。直入内，思作日月，想合径三寸许，两半放形而一，谓日月相翕者也。虽出入仍思念所作者，勿废为佳。又曰：男女俱仙之道，深内勿动精，思脐中赤色，大如鸡子形，乃徐徐出入，情动乃退。一日一夕，可数十为定，令人益寿。男女各息意，共存思之，可猛念之。御女之法，能一月再泻，一岁二十四泻，皆得二百岁，有颜色，无疾病。若加以药，则可长生也。[86p]

人年二十者四日一泻，三十者八日一泻，四十者十六日一泻，五十者二十日一泻，六十者闭精勿泻。若体力犹壮者，一月一泻。凡人气力自有盛而过人者，亦不可抑忍。久而不泻，致生痈疽。若年过六十强，有数旬不得交合，意中平平者，自可闭固也。昔正观初，有一野老，年七十余，诣余云：数日来阳气益盛，思与家妪昼寝，春事皆成，未知垂老有此为善恶耶？余答之曰：是大不祥。子独不闻膏火乎？夫膏火之将竭也，必先暗而后明，明止则灭。今足下年迈桑榆，久当闭精息欲。兹忽春情猛发，岂非反常耶？窃为足下忧之！子其勉欤！后四旬，发病而死。此其不慎之效也。如斯之辈非一。且疏一人以勖将来耳。所以善摄生者，凡觉阳事辄盛，必谨而抑之，不可纵心竭意以自贼也。若一度制得，则一度火灭，一度增油。[87p]

At twenty years old, one should release once every four days; at thirty, once every eight days; at forty, once every sixteen days; at fifty, once every twenty days; at sixty, one should refrain from release. If the body is still strong, one can release once a month. Generally, if a person's strength is naturally abundant, it should not be suppressed for too long. In the past, during the Zhengguan era, there was an old man over seventy who approached me and said: "In the past few days, my yang energy has been increasing, and I wish to sleep with my wife during the day; all spring activities have been fulfilled. I wonder if this is good or bad for an old man?" I replied: "This is very ominous. Have you not heard of the depletion of fire? When the oil is about to run out, it will first darken and then brighten; when the brightness stops, it will perish. Now, you are in the twilight of your years; you should long cease to engage your desires. Suddenly, if your spring feelings surge intensely, is that not abnormal? I am worried for you! Please take care!"

After four weeks, he fell ill and died. This was the consequence of his negligence. Such situations are not rare. I recount this to caution others in the future. Therefore, those who are adept at self-care must be careful to suppress any excessive yang energy and not allow their desires to lead them astray. If they can manage it once, they can diminish the fire once and increase the oil once.[87p]

若不能制，纵情施泻，即是膏火将灭，更去其油，可不深自防所患哉？人少年时不知道，知道亦不能信行之。至老乃知道，便已晚矣，病难养也。晚而自保，犹得延年益寿。若年少壮而能行道者，神仙速矣。或曰：年未六十，当闭精守一为可否？曰：不然。男不可无女，女不可无男。无女则意动，意动则神劳，神劳则损寿。若念真正无可思者，则大佳长生也，然而万无一有。强抑郁闭之难持易失，使人漏精尿浊，以致鬼交之病，损一而当百也。　　《古今医统》多男三炼法曰：天地闭，万物匝。男女秘，百嗣发。闭秘之法不可传，传之匪人天必罚。　　 【闭者，闭藏之义。在天地如冬时气化，畜藏不施；在人如固闭精气，一不妄泄。故万物百嗣生育之多也。[88p]

If one cannot restrain themselves and indulges excessively, it is akin to a fire that is about to extinguish; furthermore, if one continues to deplete their essence, how can they not deeply guard against the affliction? In youth, one does not understand; even when they do, they cannot trust or act upon it. Those who are young and vigorous yet can practice the path will quickly attain immortality.

Someone asks: Is it permissible to conserve one's essence and focus on singularity before reaching sixty? The answer is: No. A man cannot be without a woman, nor a woman without a man. To forcefully suppress and close off leads to difficulties in maintaining it, causing one to leak essence and urine, resulting in ailments akin to spirit interaction, diminishing one drastically.

The "Comprehensive Medical Texts" states that the method of refinement for men thrice is as follows: In the heavens and earth, there is closure; all things are enveloped. Men and women are secretive, leading to the proliferation of offspring. The method of concealment is not to be transmitted; if shared, heaven will surely punish the unworthy.

Hence, the multitude of things and offspring abounds.[88p]

此二仪阖辟之机，品物流形之妙，天人感通，生成一道，上达自能心悟，下士不可言传。】　　左右掌连心，心火暗能达。分主客，各相擦。　　 【言手心与心脉相通。右手掌擦左手心，则左为主而右为客；左手掌擦右手心，则右为主而左为客。此乃运火于脐之术。心火归脐，与肾相接合，和而不走，则坎离交媾，真元自固，而谷神可灵矣。夫谷神者，虚而能应，感而遂通者也。谷神灵则剑气刚劲，谷神弱则剑气锋委。此男女相感，机气发动，自然之妙。】　　数用重阴六十八，须知十减四七五。　　 【此相擦之数也。如一遍六十八，二遍五十八，三遍四十八，四遍三十八，五遍二十八，是擦以十减，五遍递减至四七之数也。其遍至七八九遍，皆擦二十八遍而止。】　　莫教火候过离下。[89p]

The mechanism of these two principles, their intricate transformations in the flow of existence, connects heaven and humanity in resonance, generating a single path that enables one to reach an understanding instinctively; it is beyond what can be articulated to those of lower discernment. The left and right hands connect with the heart, and the inner fire can be reached in the dark. The master and guest are differentiated and interact with each other.

This means that the palm of the hand connects with the heart channel. When the right hand’s palm rubs against the left heart, the left is the master and the right is the guest; conversely, when the left palm rubs the right heart, the right is the master and the left is the guest. This is the technique of circulating fire around the navel. The heart fire returns to the navel, connecting with the kidneys; when harmonized without dispersing, the interaction of the two oppositions leads to the solidification of the true essence, and the spirit of the valleys can respond. The spirit of the valleys is formless yet can respond, transmitting sensations effectively. When the spirit of the valleys is strong, the sword’s energy is vigorous; when it is weak, the sword’s energy falters. This mutual resonance between male and female ignites the flow of vital energy, revealing the wonders of nature.

Use the heavy Yin 68 times, and one must know to subtract 10, reducing to 47.

This refers to the number of rubs. For example, one round is 68, two rounds is 58, three rounds is 48, four rounds is 38, and five rounds is 28, representing a ten count reduction; five rounds decrease to the number of 47. When it reaches seven, eight, or nine rounds, it concludes at 28 rounds.

Do not let the timing exceed the necessary separation.[89p]

　　 【离属心，离下则属肾，言勿使火太过反动精也。】　　一擦一度伏脐间，九九老阳互相压。又知九息上增九，八十一息纯干卦。　　 【言擦一次，即将手伏压脐中，令热气入脐中。鼻中呼吸，每次九息，是息以九增。如一遍九息，二遍十八，三遍二十七，九遍渐增至八十一息也。干数用九，九九则为纯干之卦。心火属阴，故擦用重阴；肾气属阳，故息取老阳。其法于子后入室，盘坐良久，心定气平，以左手仰置左膝上，用右手心擦之六十八遍；即以左手心伏于脐间，而以右手压于左手之上，鼻中呼吸九息，用意存想，使息息归脐，此第一度。[90p]

The heart, detached, corresponds to the kidneys when lowered; one must avoid excessive heat from affecting the essence. Each stroke conducts warmth into the lower abdomen; the old yang within increases in cycles. It is known that each breath integrates into the count of nine, culminating in a total of eighty-one pure yang breaths.

This means that with each stroke, one presses the hand against the abdomen, allowing warmth to enter. Breathing through the nose, with each cycle taking nine breaths, the count increases: one round equals nine breaths, two rounds eighteen, three rounds twenty-seven, and so forth, with nine rounds gradually reaching eighty-one breaths. The number nine applies to pure yang; thus, nine times nine yields the pure yang diagram. The heart fire relates to yin, thus the strokes require strong yin; the kidney energy relates to yang, so the breaths should focus on old yang. The method is to enter a room after midnight, sit in a cross-legged position for a time, calming the heart and stabilizing the breath. With the left hand placed palm up on the left knee and the right hand rubbing it sixty-eight times; the left palm then rests on the abdomen while the right hand presses down on the left. Breathing through the nose for nine breaths, one must focus on directing the breath back to the abdomen; this constitutes the first cycle.[90p]

却以右手仰置右膝上，用左手心擦之，减十遍，即五十八遍；即以右手心伏于脐间，而以左手压于右手之上，鼻中呼吸增九息，成一十八息，亦用意存想，使息息归脐，此第二度。以后左右换手上下伏压，存想俱同，但擦以十减，压以九增，共九度而足。如此四十九日，祖气足，方可取鼎。】　　春夏秋冬名四时，二十四气尸生化，三五七九夺气机。一夺一吸深取之，周而复始天不违。　　 【此房中之术，言采夺女气之机也。三五七九皆阳数，言与女交时，但至四数，皆深入其中，上以鼻吸，下以胁提而夺取也，是女之气过我也。周而复始者，三五七九既毕，而又再从三起也。周天之数三百六十，三五七九共二十四数，以合二十四气。交时先仰行六遍，每遍二十四，得数百四十有四；后合行九遍，每遍亦二十四，得二百一十有六，共成三百六十，以合周天之数，此妙理也。仰合即天地否泰，男女上下，互相迭施之道。】　　坎水常胜离，离火易焚灭。[91p]

Then, with the right hand raised and placed on the right knee, use the left hand to rub it, reduce ten times, which makes it fifty-eight times. Then, place the right hand on the dantian (the center of the body), with the left hand pressing down on the right hand, breathing in through the nose and increasing nine breaths to make a total of eighteen breaths, using intention to focus and allow the breaths to return to the dantian; this is the second stage. Afterward, alternate hands pressing up and down, with the same intention, but reduce by ten and increase by nine for a total of nine stages. After doing this for forty-nine days, when the vital energy is sufficient, one may then take the cauldron.

The four seasons are called spring, summer, autumn, and winter, and the twenty-four solar terms are the basis of life and transformation. With each inhalation and exhalation, one deeply captures the energy, perpetually in a cycle as Heaven does not go awry.

This practice in the chamber speaks of capturing and taking the energy from a woman. The numbers three, five, seven, and nine are all odd and refer to the moments of union with a woman; however, when reaching the number four, everything penetrates deeply within. One inhales through the nose and draws up through the flanks to capture the energy of the woman, representing her energy overcoming mine. The cycle repeats, whereby once three, five, seven, and nine are completed, one begins again from three.

The number of Heaven in a cycle is three hundred sixty, and three, five, seven, and nine total twenty-four, coinciding with the twenty-four solar terms. During union, first perform the upward movement six times, each cycle being twenty-four, thus totaling four hundred forty. Afterward, perform the union nine times, each cycle also being twenty-four, resulting in two hundred sixteen, making a total of three hundred sixty, which aligns with the number of Heaven; this is the subtle principle.

The upward union signifies the harmony of Heaven and Earth, the duality of male and female, and the reciprocity of their actions.

Water in the Kan trigrams is ever-victorious, while fire in the Li trigrams can easily be extinguished.[91p]

仙草占先春，得阳阴复结。浓煎湿注参仙诀。离火纔欲然，满口莫入咽。漱无声，吐无决。暖席取溺壶，徐将肝火泻。心慵作曝蟆，虚脊凡七跌。功成敌万人，真元莫浪泄。　　 【离火易焚者，言男子之精易动。待其将动之时，即将浓浓温茗满口含之，缓漱慢吐，不可使耳闻之。又取夜壶小便以泻肝火；又作虾蟆仰曝之状，以两足两手着床席，举脊向上跌凡七次，则精即上升而不走矣。】　　要算坎，水潮生。月信进，我退投；月信退，我进接。一二炼法不可缺。更有一言须口说，左男右女肩间截。　　【言遇女子癸水生时，必俟其三日潮退，方与之交合。一二炼法，指夺气机等法而言。左男右女肩间截者，此生男之诀也。女子怀胎，在左为男，在右为女。男子将泄之精，必要向女子偏左施之。[92p]

Immortal grass takes precedence in spring, obtaining the cycles of yin and yang. Brew it strongly and immerse it, following the immortal formula. Only when离火, the fire of separation, is desired to be kindled, should nothing enter the mouth to swallow. Rinse without sound, spit without decision. Warm the seat and fetch the urinal, gently let out the liver fire. The heart, lazy like a sunbathing toad, has a hollow spine that falls seven times in total. Achieving success counters thousands, let not the true essence leak in vain.

[The fire of separation is easily ignited; this refers to how a man’s essence easily stirs. When it is about to stir, one should hold strongly brewed warm tea in the mouth, rinse slowly, and spit it out carefully, ensuring not to make any sound. Also, use a night pot to relieve liver fire; position oneself like a toad basking in the sun, with both feet and hands on the bedding, arching the spine upwards and falling seven times, then the essence will rise and not dissipate.]

One must calculate the坎, as the water tide arises. When the moon waxes, I retreat and cast; when the moon wanes, I advance to receive. The methods of one and two must not be neglected. Additionally, there is a phrase that must be spoken: "Left is for the male, right is for the female, intersecting at the shoulders."

[This states that when encountering a woman born under the heavenly water, one must wait for the tide to recede for three days before engaging in union. The one and two methods refer to techniques for seizing energy. "Left is male and right is female at the shoulders" is a secret for conceiving males. A woman carrying a child has the male on the left and the female on the right. When a man is to release his essence, it must be directed slightly to the left towards the woman.][92p]

仍以手向女子左肩上截一掌，女子左边气即上缩，精髓入左必胎男矣。】　　此是多男三炼法。六炼可长生，九炼能飞越。约尔他年逢建业。　　 【阴阳二气之运，坎离八卦之门，天地之大，尽于是焉。天地生人，物之散殊，亦尽于是焉。故离火易然，坎水易竭。阴阳动静，杂揉不剂，真元不固，谷神不灵矣。兹三炼法，《易》谓天地絪缊，万物化醇。非天人合一耶？】　　采阴诀。树衰培土，阳衰阴补。含育元气，慎莫失度。 【注云无情。】 若木至衰朽，即尘土培之。尚得再荣，又见以嫩枝接续，老树亦得长生。却为芳嫩，用意推理，阳衰阴补，是以宜之。衰阳以少阴补而不失，取其元气津液，引于我身，即颜复童矣。童男少女，正气未散，元和才一，遇之修炼，其益百倍，切忌自己元气流奔也。[93p]

With a hand, one strikes the left shoulder of the woman, causing her left qi to rise sharply, and the essence that enters the left side will lead to the conception of a boy. This is the method for cultivating many sons in the triple refinement practice. The six refinements lead to longevity, while the nine refinements allow one to transcend.

The operation of the yin and yang energies at the gate of the kan and li hexagrams encapsulates the vastness of heaven and earth. Heaven and earth give birth to humanity, and the diversity of things is also encompassed within this. Therefore, the fire of li is easily kindled, and the water of kan is easily depleted. When yin and yang interact chaotically, true essence is not stabilized, and the valley spirit becomes unresponsive. This triple refinement method is described in the Book of Changes as the essence of heaven and earth, wherein all things are transformed into purity. Is this not the unity of heaven and humanity?

The method of collecting yin: when the tree weakens, it is nourished by the earth; when yang declines, yin supplements it. One must carefully nurture the original qi and not lose measure. In commentary it is noted that there is no sentimentality. When a tree reaches decay, it is still nourished by dust to regain vitality; anew, it sprouts tender branches, allowing even an old tree to achieve longevity. Thus, using thoughtful reasoning, yang weakens while yin supplements, making this approach suitable. Weak yang is supplemented by a little yin without loss, drawing in the essence and fluids to restore vitality, resulting in a rejuvenated appearance.

For boys and girls, as their vital essence remains unscattered, and their original energy is still harmonious, encountering such cultivation yields a hundredfold benefit. It is crucial to avoid letting one's original qi flow away.[93p]

　　　　医案

　　《褚氏遗书》曰：建平王妃姬等，皆丽而无子，择良家未笄女入御，又无子。问曰：求男有道乎？澄对之曰：合男女必当其年，男虽十六而精通，必三十而娶；女虽十四而天癸至，必二十而嫁。皆欲阴阳气完实而后交合，则交而孕，孕而育，育而为子，坚壮强寿。今未笄之女，天癸始至，已近男色，阴气早泻，未完而伤，未实而动，是以交而不孕，孕而不育，育而子脆不寿。此王之所以无子也。然妇人有所产皆女者，有所产皆男者。大王诚能访求多男妇人，谋置宫府，有男之道也。王曰：善。未再期，生六男。夫老阳遇少阴，老阴遇少阳，亦有子之道也。
　　《身经通考》曰：王完虚公服万灵至宝仙酒两月，随获三胎。三仆服之，皆孕。内一人六十，妇五十二矣，已绝产念，二年亦孕，则尤异也。邹平县一人，精清无子，服之生一男。
[94p]

Medical Case

The "Chushi Yishu" states: The Princess of Jianping, Lady Ji, and others are all beautiful but without children. They selected good families for unmarried girls to enter the court, yet still had no children. It was asked: Is there a way to obtain sons? Cheng replied: For a couple, they must be of appropriate age; while a boy may be skilled at sixteen, he should marry at thirty; a girl may reach maturity at fourteen, but she should marry at twenty. They all desire the completion of yin and yang energy before they unite; thus, they conceive, give birth, and raise children, who are strong and live long. If a girl has not reached adulthood, her maturity is just beginning, already attracting male energy; her yin energy dissipates early, is incomplete, and suffers damage. Therefore, they unite but do not conceive, conceive but do not give birth, and raise children who are weak and short-lived. This is why the king has no sons. However, some women give birth only to girls, while others give birth only to boys. If the king can indeed seek many women who bear sons and plan a residence for them, there is a way to have sons. The king said: Good. Not long after, six sons were born. When the old yang encounters the young yin, and the old yin encounters the young yang, there is also a way to have children.

"The Shenjing Tongkao" states: The king took the immortal elixir of ten thousand spirits for two months and subsequently conceived three offspring. Three servants who took it all became pregnant. One of them was sixty years old, and another was fifty-two, having long since given up on the idea of childbirth, yet still became pregnant after two years, which is indeed unusual. In Zouping County, there was a man who was pure and had no children; after taking it, he fathered a son.[94p]
